	add_trait = Order_of_Military_Medal # for its actions between March-November 1918
	add_trait = Order_of_the_Crown_of_Italy # from 1918.04.30 on, he gained all the ranks of this medal
	add_trait = Legion_of_Honor # French medal gained on 1918.01.24
	add_trait = Italian_War_Cross # 1918.08.19
	add_trait = Order_of_Saint_Lazarus # held all its 3 levels in his life
	add_trait = National_medal # to simulate for the Imperial Russian 'Knight of the Order of St. Anna' title and the CZE War Cross
	add_trait = mountaineer # as he led the campaign in the Alpine region, I gave it to him
	add_trait = trickster # ex-intelligence officer
	add_trait = logistics_wizard # I'll give it to anyone who held the command of a whole Army
	add_trait = panzer_leader # led the 132a Div. Corazzata 'Ariete'
	history = {
		1937.1.1 = { rank = 1 } # actually 1937.07.01 commanding Officer of the 23a Div. Fanteria 'Murge', later-March 1939-of the 132a Div. Corazzata 'Ariete'
		1940.1.1 = { rank = 2 } # actually 1940.12.?? as commander of I. C.A., later of the V. C.A. against French troops in the Alps, the 'Comando Truppe della Tripolitania' in Lybia, then the XX. C.A.
		1943.1.1 = { rank = 3 } # actually 1943.05.03 Deputy of Chief of Staff of the Comando Supremo, 11a Armata commander before being taken prisoner by Germans
	}
